Using podAntiAffinity, specify a labelSelector that matches pods for the deployment, and set the topologyKey to kubernetes.io/hostname. Refer to https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/scheduling-eviction/assign-pod-node/#inter-pod-affinity-and-anti-affinity for details.)
